# Function that is called when trying to close the program by File/
Exit or pressing (X) button
27
def exit_program():
28
    answer = tkinter.messagebox.askquestion("SteFi", "Exit program?\
n\nAll data will be lost!",
29
                                            icon='warning')
30
    if answer == "yes":
31
        root.quit()

# Function for making default labels
181
def default_label(origin, text, x, y):
182
    label = Label(origin, text=text).place(x=x, y=y)
183
    return label

def tab_change(event):
220
    if event.widget.identify(event.x, event.y) == 'label':
221
        index = event.widget.index('@%d,%d' % (event.x, event.y))
222

223

# Area of profiles
10
def profile_area(selectedProfile, B, H, tf, tw, r, t_RHS, r1, r2, D, 
t_CHS):
11
    # Calculation
12
    if selectedProfile == "I-Profile":
13
        B = float(B); H = float(H); tf = float(tf); tw = float(tw); r
 = float(r)  # Inputs converted from string to number
14
        a = 2*B*tf+tw*(H-2*tf)+4*r**2*(1-pi/4)
15
    elif selectedProfile == "RHS":
16
        B = float(B); H = float(H); t_RHS = float(t_RHS); r1 = float(
r1); r2 = float(r2)  # Inputs converted from string to number
17
        a = (H*B-(4*r2**2*(1-pi/4))) - ((H-2*t_RHS)*(B-2*t_RHS)-(4*r1
**2*(1-pi/4)))
18
    elif selectedProfile == "CHS":
19
        D = float(D); t_CHS = float(t_CHS)  # Inputs converted from 
string to number
20
        a = (D/2)**2*pi - ((D-2*t_CHS)/2)**2*pi
21
    return a
22

# Cross section class
25
def cross_section_class(selectedProfile, P2element_type, fy, H, tw, 
r, t_RHS, r1, D, t_CHS):
26
    # Inputs converted from string to number
27
    fy = float(fy)
28
    # Calculation
29
    e = 0.85*sqrt(235/fy)
30
    if selectedProfile == "I-Profile":
31
        H = float(H); tw = float(tw); r = float(r)
32
        if P2element_type == "Beam":
33
            if (H-2*r-2*tw) / tw <= 72*e:
34
                csc = 1
35
            elif (H-2*r-2*tw) / tw <= 83*e:
36
                csc = 2
37
            elif (H-2*r-2*tw) / tw <= 124*e:
38
                csc = 3
39
            else:
40
                csc = 4
41
        elif P2element_type == "Column":
42

            if (H-2*r-2*tw) / tw <= 33*e:

            elif (H-2*r-2*tw) / tw <= 42*e:

                csc = 3

                csc = 4

    elif selectedProfile == "RHS":
52
        H = float(H); t_RHS = float(t_RHS); r1 = float(r1)

        if P2element_type == "Beam":
54
            if (H-2*r1-2*t_RHS) / t_RHS <= 72*e:

                csc = 1

# Section factor

def section_factor(selectedProfile, P2exposure_type,

    # Inputs converted from string to number

    Area = float(Area)

# Function for calculating moment of inertia
173
def moment_inertia(selectedProfile, B, H, tf, tw, r, t_RHS, r1, r2,
 D, t_CHS):
174
    # Calculation
175
==PAGE:370==
Page 5 of 24
    if selectedProfile == "I-Profile":
176
        B = float(B); H = float(H); tf = float(tf); tw = float(tw); 
r = float(r)  # Inputs converted from string to number
177
        Iy = 2* (1/12*B*tf**3+B*tf*(H/2-tf/2)**2) + 1/12*tw*(H-2*tf)
**3 + 4*(0.00742*r**4+r**2*(1-(pi/4))*(H/2-tf-0.223*r)**2)
178
        Iz = (2*(1/12*tf*B**3)+1/12*(H-2*tf)*tw**3 + 4*(0.00742*r**4
+r**2*(1-(pi/4))*(tw/2+0.223*r)**2)*4)
179
180
    elif selectedProfile == "RHS":
181
        B = float(B); H = float(H); t_RHS = float(t_RHS); r1 = float
(r1); r2 = float(r2)  # Inputs converted from string to number
182
        Iy = ((B*H**3-(B-2*t_RHS)*(H-2*t_RHS)**3)/12 + 4*(0.00742*r1
**4+r1**2*(1-(pi/4))*(H/2-t_RHS-0.223*r1)**2)
183
                   - 4*(0.00742*r2**4+r2**2*(1-(pi/4))*(H/2-0.223*r2
)**2))
184
        Iz = ((H*B**3-(H-2*t_RHS)*(B-2*t_RHS)**3)/12 + 4*(0.00742*r1
**4+r1**2*(1-(pi/4))*(B/2-t_RHS-0.223*r1)**2)
185
                   - 4*(0.00742*r2**4+r2**2*(1-(pi/4))*(B/2-0.223*r2
)**2))
186
187
    elif selectedProfile == "CHS":
188
        D = float(D); t_CHS = float(t_CHS)  # Inputs converted from
 string to number
189
        Iy = pi/64*(D**4-(D-2*t_CHS)**4)
190
        Iz = Iy
191
192
193
    return Iy, Iz

# Function for calculating section modulus
197
def section_modulus(selectedProfile, Iy, Iz, B, H, tf, tw, r, t_RHS
, r1, r2, D, t_CHS):
198
    # Inputs converted from string to number
199
    Iy = float(Iy); Iz = float(Iz)
200
    # Calculation
201
    if selectedProfile == "I-Profile":
202
        B = float(B); H = float(H); tf = float(tf); tw = float(tw); 
r = float(r)  # Inputs converted from string to number
203
        wely = Iy/(H/2)
204
        wply = B*(H*tf-tf**2) + (H/2-tf)**2*tw + 4*r**2*(1-pi/4)*(H/
2-tf-0.223*r)
205
        welz = Iz/(B/2)
206
        wplz = 1/4*H*tw**2 + (B-tw)**2*tf + 4*r**2*(1-pi/4)*(tw/2+0.
223*r)
207
208
    elif selectedProfile == "RHS":
209
        B = float(B); H = float(H); t_RHS = float(t_RHS); r1 = float
210
==PAGE:371==
Page 6 of 24
(r1); r2 = float(r2)  # Inputs converted from string to number
210
        wely = Iy/(H/2)
211
        wply = B*H*t_RHS-B*t_RHS**2 + 1/2*(H-2*t_RHS)**2*t_RHS + 4*
r1**2*(1-pi/4)*(H/2-t_RHS-0.223*r1) - 4*r2**2*(1-pi/4)*(H/2-0.223*r2
)
212
        welz = Iz/(B/2)
213
        wplz = H*B*t_RHS-H*t_RHS**2 + 1/2*(B-2*t_RHS)**2*t_RHS + 4*
r1**2*(1-pi/4)*(B/2-t_RHS-0.223*r1) - 4*r2**2*(1-pi/4)*(B/2-0.223*r2
)
214
215
    elif selectedProfile == "CHS":
216
        D = float(D); t_CHS = float(t_CHS)  # Inputs converted from
 string to number
217
        wely = Iy/(D/2)
218
        wply = (D**3-(D-2*t_CHS)**3)/6
219
        welz = wely
220
        wplz = wply
221
222
    return wely, wply, welz, wplz

# Buckling load calculation EC3 at a certain time
575
def buck_load_EC3(fy, Es, Iy, Iz, ls, Area, ky, kE, YMfi):
576
    # Inputs converted from string to number
577
    fy = float(fy); Es = float(Es)*1000; Iy = float(Iy); Iz = float(
Iz); ls = float(ls)*1000; Area = float(Area)
578
    ky = float(ky); kE = float(kE); YMfi = float(YMfi)
579
    #  Calculation
580
    alpha = 0.65*sqrt(235/fy)
581
    # Buckling load around y-axis
582
    Ncr_y = pi**2*Es*Iy/(ls**2)
583
    lambdan_y = sqrt(Area*fy/Ncr_y)
584
    lambdant_y = lambdan_y*(ky/kE)**0.5
585
    phi_y = 1/2*(1+alpha*lambdant_y+lambdant_y**2)
586
    chi_y = 1/(phi_y+sqrt(phi_y**2-lambdant_y**2))
587
    buckStressY = chi_y*ky*fy/YMfi
588
    buckLoadY = buckStressY*Area/1000
589
590
    # Buckling load around z-axis
591
    Ncr_z = pi**2*Es*Iz/(ls**2)
592
    lambdan_z = sqrt(Area*fy/Ncr_z)
593
    lambdant_z = lambdan_z*(ky/kE)**0.5
594
    phi_z = 1/2*(1+alpha*lambdant_z+lambdant_z**2)
595
    chi_z = 1/(phi_z+sqrt(phi_z**2-lambdant_z**2))
596
    buckStressZ = chi_z*ky*fy/YMfi
597
    buckLoadZ = buckStressZ*Area/1000
598
599
    return buckLoadY, buckLoadZ, buckStressY, buckStressZ

def critical_temperature_EC3(fy, Es, Iy, Iz, ls, Area, YMfi, YM0,

def parametric_fire(q, O, b):

# Eigen stresses due to temperature increase
773
def eigen_stress(selectedColumnBC2, Lb, Lb_a, Eb, Xiy, XiE, Ib, L, 
Es, Area, Ts, Load, gamma):
774
    # Inputs converted from string to number
775
    Xiy = float(Xiy); XiE = float(XiE);  L = float(L)*1000; Es = 
float(Es)*1000; Area = float(Area); Load = float(Load)*1000
776
777
==PAGE:385==
Page 20 of 24
    #  Calculation
778
    if selectedColumnBC2 == "Simple w. Simple Beam":
779
        Lb = float(Lb)*1000; Lb_a = float(Lb_a)*1000; Eb = float(Eb)
*1000; Ib = float(Ib)*1000000
780
        Lb_b = Lb - Lb_a
781
        KB = (Lb_a**2*Lb_b**2)/(3*Eb*XiE*Ib*Lb)

        gamma = 1/(1+L/(Es*XiE*Area*KB))
783
    elif selectedColumnBC2 == "Simple w. Fixed Beam":

        Lb = float(Lb)*1000; Lb_a = float(Lb_a)*1000; Eb = float(Eb)

    L_deg = (L*Load/Area)*(1/(Es*XiE)-1/Es)

    L_free = L_thermal-L_deg

# Buckling stress calculation ALT
801
def buck_load_ALT(ls, Iy, Iz, Area, fy, Xiy, XiE, Es, sigmaEigen):
802
    # Inputs converted from string to number
803
    ls = float(ls)*1000; Iy = float(Iy); Iz =float(Iz); Area = float

    XiE = float(XiE); Es = float(Es)*1000; sigmaEigen = float(

    #  Calculation

    # Buckling load around y-axis

    a_y = 1

811
    d_y = b_y**2-4*a_y*c_y

    buckStressY = ((-b_y-sqrt(d_y))/2*a_y)-sigmaEigen

    buckLoadY = buckStressY*Area/1000

    # Buckling load around z-axis
816
    lambda_z = ls/sqrt(Iz/Area)

    a_z = 1

    buckLoadZ = buckStressZ*Area/1000

def limit_load(selectedBeamBC, Wply, fy, L):

    # Inputs converted from strings to numbers

    Wply = float(Wply); fy = float(fy) ; L = float(L)

        Plim20 = ((6*Wply*fy)/(L*1000))/1000  # [kN]

    # Inputs converted from strings to numbers

    Wely = float(Wely); fy = float(fy); L = float(L)
855
856
    if selectedBeamBC == "Simply supported (Point)":
857
        Pel = ((4*Wely*fy)/(L*1000))/1000  # [kN]
858
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Simple/Fixed (Point)":
859
        Pel = ((16*Wely*fy)/(3*L*1000))/1000  # [kN]
860
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Fixed ends (Point)":
861
        Pel = ((8*Wely*fy)/(L*1000))/1000  # [kN]
862
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Cantilever (Point)":
863
        Pel = ((Wely*fy)/(L*1000))/1000  # [kN]
864
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Simply supported (Uniform)":
865
        Pel = (8*Wely*fy)/((L*1000)**2)  # [kN/m]
866
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Simple/Fixed (Uniform)":
867
        Pel = (8*Wely*fy)/((L*1000)**2)  # [kN/m]
868
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Fixed ends (Uniform)":
869
==PAGE:387==
Page 22 of 24
        Pel = (12*Wely*fy)/((L*1000)**2)  # [kN/m]
870
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Cantilever (Uniform)":
871
        Pel = (2*Wely*fy)/((L*1000)**2)  # [kN/m]

    return Pel

# Function for finding the plastic load (P1)
876
def plastic_load(selectedBeamBC, Wply, fy, L):
877
    # Inputs converted from strings to numbers
878
    Wply = float(Wply); fy = float(fy); L = float(L)
879
880
    if selectedBeamBC == "Simply supported (Point)":
881
        P1 = ((4*Wply*fy)/(L*1000))/1000  # [kN]
882
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Simple/Fixed (Point)":
883
        P1 = ((16*Wply*fy)/(3*L*1000))/1000  # [kN]
884
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Fixed ends (Point)":
885
        P1 = ((8*Wply*fy)/(L*1000))/1000  # [kN]
886
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Cantilever (Point)":
887
        P1 = ((Wply*fy)/(L*1000))/1000  # [kN]
888
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Simply supported (Uniform)":
889
        P1 = (8*Wply*fy)/((L*1000)**2)  # [kN/m]
890
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Simple/Fixed (Uniform)":
891
        P1 = (8*Wply*fy)/((L*1000)**2)  # [kN/m]
892
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Fixed ends (Uniform)":
893
        P1 = (12*Wply*fy)/((L*1000)**2)  # [kN/m]
894
    elif selectedBeamBC == "Cantilever (Uniform)":
895
        P1 = (2*Wply*fy)/((L*1000)**2)  # [kN/m]
896
    return P1

# Critical temperature ALT
900
def critical_temperature_ALT(P2element_type, selectedBeamBC, Wply, 
Wely, fy, L, Load, selectedColumnBC2, Lb,
901
                             Lb_a, Eb, Ib, Es, Area, ls, Iy, Iz, 
Xiycr, XiEcr, gamma):
902
    temperature = 0
903
    if P2element_type == "Beam":
904
        Load = float(Load)
905
        Plim20 = limit_load(selectedBeamBC, Wply, fy, L)
906
        Pel = elastic_load(selectedBeamBC, Wely, fy, L)
907
        P1 = plastic_load(selectedBeamBC, Wply, fy, L)
908
        R = Plim20 / P1
909
        Zeta = P1 / Pel
910
        for i in range(len(Xiycr)):
911
            Beta = R*Zeta*Xiycr[i]
912
            Pcr = (round(Beta * Pel, 3))
913
            if Load > Pcr:
914
                Tcry = temperature - 0.1
915
==PAGE:388==
Page 23 of 24
                break
916
            else:
917
                temperature = temperature + 0.1
918
        temp = [Tcry, 20, 0]
919
920
    elif P2element_type == "Column":
921
        fy = float(fy); Es = float(Es)*1000; Load = float(Load)*1000
; L = float(L)*1000; ls = float(ls)*1000; Area = float(Area)
922
        Iy = float(Iy); Iz = float(Iz)
923
        if selectedColumnBC2 == "Simple w. Simple Beam" or 
selectedColumnBC2 == "Simple w. Fixed Beam":
924
            Lb = float(Lb)*1000; Lb_a = float(Lb_a)*1000; Eb = float
(Eb)*1000; Ib = float(Ib)*1000000
925
            Lb_b = Lb - Lb_a
926
927
        y = 0  # variable to only get the lowest critical 
temperature
928
        z = 0  # variable to only get the lowest critical 
temperature
929
        for i in range(len(Xiycr)):
930
            if selectedColumnBC2 == "Simple w. Simple Beam":
931
                KB = (Lb_a**2*Lb_b**2) / (3*Eb*XiEcr[i]*Ib*Lb)
932
                gamma = 1 / (1 + L / (Es*XiEcr[i]*Area*KB))
933
            elif selectedColumnBC2 == "Simple w. Fixed Beam":
934
                KB = (Lb_a**3*Lb_b**3) / (3*Eb*XiEcr[i]*Ib*Lb**3)
935
                gamma = 1 / (1 + L / (Es*XiEcr[i]*Area*KB))
936
            else:
937
                gamma = float(gamma)
938
939
            alpha = 11.75*10**-6
940
            L_thermal = alpha*temperature*L
941
            L_deg = (L * Load/Area) * (1/(Es*XiEcr[i]) - 1/Es)
942
            L_free = L_thermal - L_deg
943
            eigenStress = Es * XiEcr[i] * (1-gamma) * L_free/L
944
945
            # Buckling load around y-axis
946
            lambda_y = ls/sqrt(Iy/Area)
947
            a_y = 1
948
            b_y = -1*((fy*Xiycr[i])+pi**2*Es*XiEcr[i]*(4.8*10**(-5)+
1/(lambda_y**2)))
949
            c_y = fy*Xiycr[i]*(pi**2*Es*XiEcr[i]) / (lambda_y**2)
950
            d_y = b_y**2-4*a_y*c_y
951
            buckStressY = ((-b_y-sqrt(d_y)) / 2*a_y) - eigenStress
952
            buckLoadY = buckStressY * Area
953
954
            # Buckling load around z-axis
955
            lambda_z = ls/sqrt(Iz/Area)
956
            a_z = 1
957
==PAGE:389==
Page 24 of 24
            b_z = -1*((fy*Xiycr[i])+pi**2*Es*XiEcr[i]*(4.8*10**(-5)
+1/(lambda_z**2)))
958
            c_z = fy*Xiycr[i]*(pi**2*Es*XiEcr[i]) / (lambda_z**2)
959
            d_z = b_z**2 - 4*a_z*c_z
960
            buckStressZ = ((-b_z-sqrt(d_z)) / 2*a_z) - eigenStress
961
            buckLoadZ = buckStressZ*Area
962
963
            if Load > buckLoadY and y == 0:
964
                Tcry = temperature - 0.1
965
                y = 1
966
                temperature = temperature + 0.1
967
            elif Load > buckLoadZ and z == 0:
968
                Tcrz =temperature - 0.1
969
                z = 1
970
                temperature = temperature + 0.1
971
            elif y == 0 or z == 0:
972
                temperature = temperature + 0.1
973
            else:
974
                break
975
976
        temp = [Tcry, Tcrz, gamma]
977
    return temp
